< review>
We took a break at Dinosaur Park for the kids after riding our bikes and e-scooters on the Aliso Creek bike trail and the place was nice and clean. I like that there is a smaller separate playground area for young toddlers and a bigger separate area for older kids. All the playground equipment looked well-maintained and the kids had fun playing on the slides, swing, and the sand.

The only bad thing about this place was that all the bathrooms were closed (locked) and one had to use a porta-potty located far off (probably due to COVID-19).

Also, despite signs asking parents and kids to wear face coverings, about 95% of the people here did not wear any masks (kids & adults).

During normal circumstances, this park would be a great place for both adults and kids to relax and play.</review>

< review>
So fun, safely located (far from the street), and there's a good bathroom! I loved it when I only had 1 little kid and 1 baby. However, it's too difficult to manage with 3 young kids. It's 2 levels and you can't see much of the other from whichever one you're on. And there's a water play feature made of cement, just the right height to be climbed onto and very fun, but a slippery and messy hazard if an adult isn't right there next to it. I wish they would just put a little fence around the water area. And because kids can get out of sight and lost easily, I only go if I have another adult to bring with me.<//review>

< review>
I used to really love this park. Was Colony Mobile Home Park, now is Hometown America Colonial
Estates. They put up an entrance gate then it became 'Estates'.
We had a very friendly community, but our residents got older, died or moved away.
Take a 'short putt' inside and count the amount of empty lots and 'for sale signs' and ask yourself:
WHY ? ? ?
The clubhouse is very well kept...But it seems to not be in much use..
I myself am very disappointed as to the present attitude and concern from the residents and site
management of the health of the community.
I have lived here approx. 20 years. I and my wife as well of most of my neighbors are disabled or are
'Dirt Poor'. It is a struggle to tolerate some of the 'attitude' going on...Perhaps it is ME or the 'sign of the times'...The 'buck($)' seems to be the question and answer, I have neither...</review>

<Review>Worst experience I have ever had with any property mangament company!!!! From the rental property to the customer service this business is by far the worst business.

I have only been in this rental property house for 6 days and I have numerous incidents and issues already.

This high end rental house ($4400 per month) was advertised as "move in ready" which clearly was not move in ready. The day I moved in I found out the refrigerator was broken and a new one was to be delivered the next day. I drove 4 hours to get here and I had groceries that needed to be refrigerated. I ended up throwing 3 large bags of food away. The communication was very poor from Mangold Property Management. If they knew the refrigerator was broken the day before I came they could have called/emailed me and informed me that a the refrigerator was broken, a new one was coming in a couple of days and not to pack any perishable items for there is no place to store them. I could have given my 3 bags of food away rather than packing it and letting it spoil.

Besides the broken refrigerator there was no microwave in the kitchen. 6 days ago when I signed my lease I was told a microwave should be coming but they had no clue when it is suppose to get here. 6 days later and still no word on the microwave.
